Middleware likely cannot log the root path because the basePath is set to `/monitor`. This makes instrumentation ineffective for this specific 404.

I will apply the redirect fix now. The curl results and code comparison with web-admin provide 100% confidence. Complex instrumentation is unnecessary.

I will hold off on the redirect fix. I need to instrument the app first to capture the 404 behavior. Next.js middleware may still match the root path despite basePath. I will ask the user to reproduce the error after instrumentation is in place.

## 问题分析

`GET http://localhost:3003/` 返回 404 是**预期行为**，不是服务没启动。

`web-monitor` 在 `next.config.mjs` 里配置了 `basePath: '/monitor'`，页面实际挂载在 `/monitor` 下，而不是根路径 `/`。Nginx 也是按 `/monitor` 代理的。

### 假设验证（运行时证据）

| 假设 | 结论 | 证据 |
|------|------|------|
| **A** `basePath` 导致 `/` 无路由 | **已确认** | `curl /` → 404；`curl /monitor` → 200；日志 `pathname: "/"` |
| **B** 3003 端口不是 web-monitor | **排除** | 响应头 `X-Powered-By: Next.js` |
| **C** `page.tsx` 缺失或损坏 | **排除** | `/monitor` 正常返回 200 |
| **D** 代理/Nginx 路径被截断 | **排除** | 直连 localhost 同样 404 |
| **D** dev 服务未启动 | **排除** | 端口有响应 |

对比 `web-admin`（`basePath: '/admin'`），它已配置了根路径重定向，而 `web-monitor` 之前缺少同样配置。

## 已做修复

在 `apps/web-monitor/next.config.mjs` 中增加了与 `web-admin` 一致的重定向：`/` → `/monitor`。

访问方式：
- **修复前**：需手动打开 `http://localhost:3003/monitor`
- **修复后**：`http://localhost:3003/` 会自动跳转到 `/monitor`

**注意**：修改 `next.config.mjs` 后需要**重启** web-monitor dev 服务才能生效。

<reproduction_steps>
1. 停止当前 web-monitor 开发服务（若通过 `pnpm dev` / `turbo dev` 运行，先 Ctrl+C 停掉）
2. 重新启动：`cd apps/web-monitor && pnpm dev`，或在项目根目录运行 `pnpm dev`
3. 浏览器访问 `http://localhost:3003/`，应自动跳转到 `/monitor` 并显示监控看板
4. 也可直接访问 `http://localhost:3003/monitor` 作为备用入口
5. Press Proceed/Mark as fixed when done.
</reproduction_steps>

帮我把 localhost:3000 默认路由到 /monitor

## 助手

  "result": "{\"contents\":\"'use client';\\n\\nimport { useCallback, useEffect, useState } from 'react';\\nimport { Button, Input, Modal, Select, Space, Table, Tag, message } from 'antd';\\nimport { AdminLayout } from '../../components/AdminLayout';\\nimport { alertApi, type AlertItem } from '../../lib/api';\\n\\nconst LEVEL_COLOR: Record<string, string> = {\\n  info: 'default',\\n  warning: 'orange',\\n  error: 'red',\\n  critical: 'magenta',\\n};\\n\\nconst STATUS_LABEL: Record<string, string> = {\\n  open: '未读',\\n  acknowledged: '已读',\\n  resolved: '已处理',\\n};\\n\\nexport default function AlertsPage() {\\n  const [items, setItems] = useState<AlertItem[]>([]);\\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);\\n  const [statusFilter, setStatusFilter] = useState<string | undefined>();\\n  const [levelFilter, setLevelFilter] = useState<string | undefined>();\\n  const [selected, setSelected] = useState<string[]>([]);\\n  const [resolveOpen, setResolveOpen] = useState(false);\\n  const [resolveId, setResolveId] = useState<string | null>(null);\\n  const [note, setNote] = useState('');\\n\\n  const load = useCallback(async () => {\\n    setLoading(true);\\n    try {\\n      const query: Record<string, string> = {};\\n      if (statusFilter) query.status = statusFilter;\\n      if (levelFilter) query.level = levelFilter;\\n      const data = await alertApi.list(Object.keys(query).length ? query : undefined);\\n      setItems(data.items);\\n    } catch (err) {\\n      message.error(err instanceof Error ? err.message : '加载失败');\\n    } finally {\\n      setLoading(false);\\n    }\\n  }, [statusFilter, levelFilter]);\\n\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    load();\\n  }, [load]);\\n\\n  const onBatchRead = async () => {\\n    if (selected.length === 0) return;\\n    try {\\n      await alertApi.batchRead(selected);\\n      message.success('已批量标记已读');\\n      setSelected([]);\\n      load();\\n    } catch (err) {\\n      message.error(err instanceof Error ? err.message : '操作失败');\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const onResolve = async () => {\\n    if (!resolveId) return;\\n    try {\\n      await alertApi.update(resolveId, { status: 'resolved', resolutionNote: note || undefined });\\n      message.success('已标记为已处理');\\n      setResolveOpen(false);\\n      setNote('');\\n      load();\\n    } catch (err) {\\n      message.error(err instanceof Error ? err.message : '操作失败');\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  return (\\n    <AdminLayout>\\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: 16 }}>\\n        <div>\\n          <h1 style={{ fontSize: 18, margin: 0 }}>告警信息</h1>\\n          <p style={{ color: '#64748B', margin: '4px 0 0' }}>与监控看板同源的事件列表与处置闭环</p>\\n        </div>\\n        <Space>\\n          <Select\\n            allowClear\\n            placeholder=\\\"处理状态\\\"\\n            style={{ width: 120 }}\\n            value={statusFilter}\\n            onChange={setStatusFilter}\\n            options={[\\n              { value: 'open', label: '未读' },\\n              { value: 'acknowledged', label: '已读' },\\n              { value: 'resolved', label: '已处理' },\\n            ]}\\n          />\\n          <Select\\n            allowClear\\n            placeholder=\\\"级别\\\"\\n            style={{ width: 120 }}\\n            value={levelFilter}\\n            onChange={setLevelFilter}\\n            options={[\\n              { value: 'warning', label: '中' },\\n              { value: 'error', label: '高' },\\n              { value: 'critical', label: '严重' },\\n            ]}\\n          />\\n          <Button disabled={selected.length === 0} onClick={onBatchRead}>\\n            批量已读\\n          </Button>\\n        </Space>\\n      </div>\\n\\n      <Table\\n        rowKey=\\\"id\\\"\\n        loading={loading}\\n        dataSource={items}\\n        rowSelection={{\\n          selectedRowKeys: selected,\\n          onChange: (keys) => setSelected(keys as string[]),\\n        }}\\n        columns={[\\n          {\\n            title: '级别',\\n            dataIndex: 'level',\\n            render: (v: string) => <Tag color={LEVEL_COLOR[v]}>{v}</Tag>,\\n          },\\n          { title: '类型', dataIndex: 'type' },\\n          { title: '摘要', dataIndex: 'title' },\\n          {\\n            title: '状态',\\n            dataIndex: 'status',\\n            render: (v: string) => STATUS_LABEL[v] ?? ## 问题分析

| 假设 | 结论 | 证据 |
|------|------|------|
| **A** 链接缺少 `basePath: '/admin'` | **已确认** | `curl /alerts` → 404；`curl /admin/alerts` → 200 |
| **B** 告警页不存在 | **排除** | `apps/web-admin/app/alerts/page.tsx` 存在 |
| **C** 端口错误 | **排除** | 3002 上 Next.js 正常响应 |

监控看板里硬编码了 `http://localhost:3002/alerts?id=...`，但管理端实际路由是 `/admin/alerts`（与 `web-admin` 的 `basePath` 一致）。

## 已做修复

1. **`apps/web-monitor/app/lib/api.ts`** — 新增 `adminAlertUrl()`，生成正确链接：`http://localhost:3002/admin/alerts?id=...`
2. **`apps/web-monitor/app/page.tsx`** — 告警详情链接改用 `adminAlertUrl()`
3. **`apps/web-admin/app/alerts/page.tsx`** — 支持 `?id=` 参数，自动高亮并提示对应告警
4. **`.env.example`** — 新增 `NEXT_PUBLIC_ADMIN_URL` 配置项

## 验证结果

- `curl http://localhost:3002/admin/alerts?id=...` → **200 OK**
- `adminAlertUrl` 单元测试 → **3 passed**

<reproduction_steps>
1. 若 web-monitor / web-admin 开发服务已在运行，刷新页面即可（修改 next.config 才需重启；本次改动支持热更新）
2. 打开监控看板 `http://localhost:3003/monitor`，在检索质量预警区域点击「查看管理端告警详情」
3. 确认跳转到 `http://localhost:3002/admin/alerts?id=...`（注意 URL 中有 `/admin`），页面正常显示告警列表
4. 若 URL 带 `id` 参数，对应告警行应高亮并弹出定位提示
5. Press Proceed/Mark as fixed when done.
</reproduction_steps>
